            var bnnr_no;
            
            if (randingBnMain.length > 0) {
                var randingBnNum = Math.floor(Math.random() * (randingBnMain.length));
                $("#dev_landingBn").css("background", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].background);
                $("#dev_landingBn a").attr("href", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].url);
                $("#dev_landingBn a").attr("target", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].target);
                $("#dev_landingBn a>img").attr("src", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].src);
                $("#dev_landingBn a>img").attr("alt", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].alt);
                bnnr_no = randingBnMain[randingBnNum].bnnr_no;
            }
            

            function landingBnClickCnt() {
                albamontargetURL.location.href = "/etc/gnbtopbn_cnt.asp?bnnr_no=" + bnnr_no;
            }

            $(function () {
                    
                if (randingBnMain.length > 0) {
                    var randingBnCookie = getCookie("dev_randingBnMain20131015");
                    if (randingBnCookie != null) {
                        $("#dev_landingBn").hide();
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#dev_landingBn").slideDown(400, function () {
                            $("#div_fly_right").css('top', '300px');
                        });

                        $("#dev_landingBn button").click(function () {
                            var nowDate = new Date();
                            var nowHours = nowDate.getHours();
                            var nowMinutes = nowDate.getMinutes();
                            var cookie_time = (60 * (24 * 7)) - (nowHours * 60 + nowMinutes); // 7일
                            setCookie('dev_randingBnMain20131015', 'yes', cookie_time, '/', 'albamon.com');
                            $("#dev_landingBn").hide();
                        });
                    }
                }
                
            });
        </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var gnbiPv2 = Math.ceil(Math.random() * $('#dev_gnbNotice2 li').length - 1);
    var gnbFixedStat = "0";
    gnbiBinit(gnbiPv2, 'dev_gnbNotice2');

    //-- GNB fixed Set - - - - 
    $(window).load(function () {
        if ($.trim(gnbFixedStat) == "1") {
            // 새로고침 했을 경우를 대비한 메소드 실행
            scrollController();

            // 스크롤을 하는 경우에만 실행됨
            $(window).scroll(function () {
                scrollController();
            });

            // 메뉴 가릴경우 뿔 아이콘 제거
            $(window).resize(function () {
                if ($("div.secNavWrap").hasClass("secNavWrap_1")) {
                    if ($(window).width() <= 1050) {
                        $('.secNavWrap .albamonIcon').removeClass('on');
                    } else {
                        $('.secNavWrap .albamonIcon').addClass('on');
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    });

    // 메인 메뉴의 위치를 제어하는 함수
    function scrollController() {
        currentScrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
        if (currentScrollTop < 130) {
            $("div.secNavWrap").removeClass("secNavWrap_1");
            $('.secNavWrap .albamonIcon').removeClass('on');
        } else {
            $("div.secNavWrap").addClass("secNavWrap_1");
            if ($(window).width() > 1000) {
                $('.secNavWrap .albamonIcon').addClass('on');
            }
        }
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    DrawSbanner();
    function DrawSbanner() {
        var $alink = "";
        if (arySbanner1 != null && arySbanner1.length > 0) {
            arySbanner1.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
            $alink = $(arySbanner1[0].StrHtml);
        }
        else
            $alink= $("<a href='/service/campaign/' target='_blank'><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/point/bl_line_1.gif' alt='바람직한 채용문화 함께 만들어요' /></a>");

        $alink.appendTo(".bl_1");

        if (arySbanner2 != null && arySbanner2.length > 0) {
            arySbanner2.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
            $alink = $(arySbanner2[0].StrHtml);
        }
        else
            $alink = $("<span id='dev_bnnr1'><a href='http://www.albamon.com/service/company/award_rank.asp' target='_blank'><img src='http://file3.jobkorea.co.kr/albamon/notice/Mon_20130423_2.jpg' alt='랭키닷컴 아르바이트 사이트 순위 1위' width='240' height='145' /></a></span>");

        $alink.appendTo(".bl_2");
    }


    function set_count(alink, idx) {
        $.ajax({
            url: "/Main/Etc/sbanner_view_cnt?idx=" + idx,
            type: "GET",
            error: function (info, xhr) {
                location.href = alink.href;
            },
            success: function (req) {
            }
        });
    }

    function bnnr_count(bnnr_no) {
        $.ajax({
            url: "/Main/Etc/bnnr_cnt",
            type: 'post',
            data: { bnnr_no: bnnr_no },
            dataType: 'text',
            success: function (data) { return; },
            error: function () {
                return; //에러
            }
        });
    }

</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            var vTickerlist;
            var NotShowMemFlag = "2";
            $.get('/Main/Login/getMemTypeCode', function (result) {
                //기업 C, 개인 M, 비로그인 N
                if (result) {
                    if ($.trim(result) == "C") {
                        NotShowMemFlag = "1";
                    }

                    if ($.trim(result) != "N") {    //비로그인은 모두다 노출
                        $("#dev_mainNotice ul li[reg_group=" + NotShowMemFlag + "]").each(function () {
                            $(this).remove();
                        });
                    }

                    vTickerlist = $('#dev_mainNotice').find("a");
                    $('#dev_mainNotice').vTicker({
                        // 스크롤 속도(default: 700)
                        speed: 500,
                        // 스크롤 사이의 대기시간(default: 4000)
                        pause: 3000,
                        // 스크롤 애니메이션
                        animation: 'fade',
                        // 마우스 over 일때 멈출 설정
                        mousePause: true,
                        // 한번에 보일 리스트수(default: 2)
                        showItems: 1,
                        // 스크롤 컨테이너 높이(default: 0)
                        height: 0,
                        // 아이템이 움직이는 방향, up/down (default: up)
                        direction: 'up'
                    });

                    $(vTickerlist).focus(function () { $('#dev_mainNotice').vTicker('pause', true); });
                    $(vTickerlist).blur(function () { $('#dev_mainNotice').vTicker('pause', false); });
                }
            });
          
			function vTickerPause(isPause){
				$('#dev_mainNotice').vTicker('pause', isPause);
			}
        </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    Draw();

    function Draw() {
        aryPlatinumVIP.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
        aryPlatinumGod_F.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
        aryPlatinumGod.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
        aryPlatinum.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });

        var PlatinumVIPBigBanner = BannerCnt;
        var aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList = aryPlatinumVIP.splice(0, PlatinumVIPBigBanner);
                
            var aryStaticImage = ["a1", "a2", "a3", "a4", "a5", "a6"];
            

        aryStaticImage.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
        var $ul = $(".vip");
        var $ul_G = $(".platinumWrap .gold");
        var $ul_B = $("#dev_opt_platinum .base"); //플래티넘의 디폴트 박스
        var divideNumB = 5;

        var PlatinumFormat = [];
        PlatinumFormat.push("<li {0}>");
        PlatinumFormat.push("   <dl>");
        PlatinumFormat.push("       <dt>{1}{2}<span class='logo'>{3}</span></a></dt>");
        PlatinumFormat.push("       <dd class='tit'>{4}</dd>");
        PlatinumFormat.push("       <dd class='etc'><span>{5}</span><span class='pay'>{6}</span></dd>");
        PlatinumFormat.push("       <dd class='vBtn'>{7}</dd>");
        PlatinumFormat.push("   </dl>");
        PlatinumFormat.push("   {8}");
        PlatinumFormat.push("</li>");

        var VipBanner = "";
        var Vip = "";
        var Gold = "";
        var Gold_F = "";
        var Base = "";

        if (aryPlatinumVIP.length + PlatinumVIPBigBanner > 0) {
            //플래티넘VIP 빅배너
            for (var i = 0; i < PlatinumVIPBigBanner; i++) {

                VipBanner = PlatinumFormat.join("");

                if (aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].bgImg != "" && aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].type == "PF")
                    VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{0}", "class='fsVip' style=\"background: #FFF url('" + aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].bgImg + "') no-repeat center top\" ");
                else
                    VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{0}", " class='fsVip " + aryStaticImage.pop() + "'");

                VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{1}", "");

                if (aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].type == "PF")
                    VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{7}", aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].strLink + "<span>채용관 바로가기</span></a>");
                else
                    VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{7}", "<button type='button' class='pView pgSimpleGI' id='pgSimpleImgPL_" + aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].alGINo + "' optgcd ='" + aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].clickCount + "'>미리보기</button>" + aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].strLink + "<span>지원하기</span></a>" + aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].strLink + "지원하기</a>");

                VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{2}", aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].strLink + aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].c_name);
                VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{3}", aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].strImg);
                VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{4}", aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].strSubjectClass);
                VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{5}", aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].dutyGuCode);
                VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{6}", aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].strPay);
                VipBanner = VipBanner.replace("{8}", "");
                var $VipBanner = $(VipBanner);

                if (aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList[i].type != "PF") {
                    $VipBanner.find(".vBtn > a:eq(0)").addClass("dView");
                    $VipBanner.find(".vBtn > a:eq(1)").addClass("scp");
                }
                else
                    $VipBanner.find(".vBtn > a").addClass("pGo");

                $VipBanner.appendTo($ul);
            }

            //플래티넘VIP
            for (var i = 0; i < aryPlatinumVIP.length; i++) {

                Vip = PlatinumFormat.join("");

                Vip = Vip.replace("{0}", "class='dev_Franchise_v'");
                Vip = Vip.replace("{1}", "");
                Vip = Vip.replace("{2}", aryPlatinumVIP[i].strLink + aryPlatinumVIP[i].c_name);
                Vip = Vip.replace("{3}", aryPlatinumVIP[i].strImg);
                Vip = Vip.replace("{4}", aryPlatinumVIP[i].strSubjectClass);
                Vip = Vip.replace("{5}", aryPlatinumVIP[i].dutyGuCode);
                Vip = Vip.replace("{6}", aryPlatinumVIP[i].strPay);


                if (aryPlatinumVIP[i].type != "PF") {
                    Vip = Vip.replace("{7}", "<button type='button' class='smr pgSimpleGI' id='pgSimpleImgPL_" + aryPlatinumVIP[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + aryPlatinumVIP[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");
                    Vip = Vip.replace("{8}", "");
                }
                else {
                    Vip = Vip.replace("{7}", "");
                    Vip = Vip.replace("{8}", aryPlatinumVIP[i].strLayer);
                }

                var $Vip = $(Vip);
                $Vip.find(".vBtn").removeClass().addClass("bv");

                $Vip.appendTo($ul);
            }


            //빈상품영역
            var VIPtotalCnt = aryPlatinumVIPBIGBannerList.length + aryPlatinumVIP.length + parseInt(PlatinumVIPBigBanner); //백배너는 2개로 생각한다.
            if (VIPtotalCnt % divideNumB != 0 || VIPtotalCnt < 10) {
                var $ul_B_vip = $("#dev_opt_platinumVIP .base");
                var cnt = (divideNumB - (parseInt(VIPtotalCnt) % divideNumB));

                //박스갯수에 따라 노출되는 빈박스 달라진다.
                //박스영역에 빈박스 상품을 채워야된다면..
                if (VIPtotalCnt < 10)
                    cnt = 10 - VIPtotalCnt;

                for (var i = 0; i < cnt; i++) {
                    var $li = $("<li class='noneVip'></li>");
                    $li.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=PlatinumVIP&utm_source=blank_banner&utm_medium=click&utm_campaign=pletinumVIP','','');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_platinumVIP_1.gif' alt='M 점프, 파워점프, 지역 Grand, 지역 TOP-Logo, 업직종 TOP-Logo 무료, 상품안내 및 신청'/></a>");
                    $li.appendTo($ul_B_vip);
                }
            }
        } else {
            var $ul_B_vip = $("#dev_opt_platinumVIP .base");
            for (var i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
                var $li = $("<li class='noneVip'></li>");
                $li.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=PlatinumVIP&utm_source=blank_banner&utm_medium=click&utm_campaign=pletinumVIP','','');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_platinumVIP_1.gif' alt='M 점프, 파워점프, 지역 Grand, 지역 TOP-Logo, 업직종 TOP-Logo 무료, 상품안내 및 신청'/></a>");
                $li.appendTo($ul_B_vip);
            }
        }

        //플래티넘 골드
        var TotalLoopBG = aryPlatinumGod.length + aryPlatinumGod_F.length;
        if (TotalLoopBG > 0) {
            //플래티넘 골드노출
            for (var i = 0; i < aryPlatinumGod.length; i++) {
                Gold = PlatinumFormat.join("");

                if (aryPlatinumGod[i].bgColor == "2")
                    Gold = Gold.replace("{0}", "class='bgc'");
                else
                    Gold = Gold.replace("{0}", "");

                Gold = Gold.replace("{2}", aryPlatinumGod[i].strLink + aryPlatinumGod[i].c_name);
                Gold = Gold.replace("{7}", "<button type='button' class='smr pgSimpleGI' id='pgSimpleImgPL_" + aryPlatinumGod[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + aryPlatinumGod[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");
                Gold = Gold.replace("{8}", "");

                Gold = Gold.replace("{1}", "");
                Gold = Gold.replace("{3}", aryPlatinumGod[i].strImg);
                Gold = Gold.replace("{4}", aryPlatinumGod[i].strSubjectClass);
                Gold = Gold.replace("{5}", aryPlatinumGod[i].dutyGuCode);
                Gold = Gold.replace("{6}", aryPlatinumGod[i].strPay);

                var $Gold = $(Gold);

                $Gold.find(".vBtn").removeClass().addClass("bv");
                $Gold.appendTo($ul_G);
            }

            //플래티넘 프랜차이즈 노출
            for (var i = 0; i < aryPlatinumGod_F.length; i++) {
                Gold_F = PlatinumFormat.join("");

                if (aryPlatinumGod_F[i].strLayer == "")
                    Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{0}", "");
                else
                    Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{0}", "class='dev_Franchise_c'");


                if (aryPlatinumGod_F[i].flags_code == "36")
                    Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{2}", "<a href='/list/gi/mon_store_CJ_intro.asp' target='_blank' >CJ푸드빌");
                else
                    Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{2}", aryPlatinumGod_F[i].strLink + aryPlatinumGod_F[i].c_name);

                Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{7}", "");
                Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{8}", aryPlatinumGod_F[i].strLayer);


                Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{1}", "");
                Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{3}", aryPlatinumGod_F[i].strImg);
                Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{4}", aryPlatinumGod_F[i].strSubjectClass);
                Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{5}", aryPlatinumGod_F[i].dutyGuCode);
                Gold_F = Gold_F.replace("{6}", aryPlatinumGod_F[i].strPay);

                var $Gold_F = $(Gold_F);

                $Gold_F.find(".vBtn").removeClass().addClass("bv");
                $Gold_F.appendTo($ul_G);
            }
        }

        //플래티넘 일반
        var BaseCnt = aryPlatinum.length;
        if (parseInt(BaseCnt) > 0) {
            for (var i = 0; i < BaseCnt; i++) {
                Base = PlatinumFormat.join("");
                if (aryPlatinum[i].bgColor == "2")
                    Base = Base.replace("{0}", "class='bgc'")
                else
                    Base = Base.replace("{0}", "")

                Base = Base.replace("{1}", "");
                Base = Base.replace("{2}", aryPlatinum[i].strLink + aryPlatinum[i].c_name);
                Base = Base.replace("{3}", aryPlatinum[i].strImg);
                Base = Base.replace("{4}", aryPlatinum[i].strSubjectClass);
                Base = Base.replace("{5}", aryPlatinum[i].dutyGuCode);
                Base = Base.replace("{6}", aryPlatinum[i].strPay);
                Base = Base.replace("{7}", "<button type='button' class='smr pgSimpleGI' id='pgSimpleImgPL_" + aryPlatinum[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + aryPlatinum[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");
                Base = Base.replace("{8}", "");

                var $Base = $(Base);
                $Base.find(".vBtn").removeClass().addClass("bv");
                $Base.appendTo($ul_B);
            }
        }

        //빈상품영역
        var totalCnt = aryPlatinumGod.length + aryPlatinumGod_F.length + aryPlatinum.length;
        DrawBanner(totalCnt);

    }

    function DrawBanner(totalcnt) {
        var divideNumB = 5;
        if (totalcnt % divideNumB != 0) {
            var $ul_B = $("#dev_opt_platinum .base");
            var cnt = (divideNumB - (parseInt(totalcnt) % divideNumB));
            for (var i = 0; i < cnt; i++) {
                var $li = $("<li class='none'></li>");
                $li.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Platinum&utm_source=main&utm_medium=click&utm_campaign=pletinum','','');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_platinum_1.gif' alt='파워점프, 지역Grand, 지역 TOP-Logo, 업직종 TOP-Logo 무료 상품안내 및 신청'/></a>");
                $li.appendTo($ul_B);
            }
        }
    }

<script type="text/javascript">

    //메인 상품 안내 레이어 창
    $(function () {
        $(".dev_guinoptinfo")
			.click(function (e) {
			    var mflag = $(this).attr("id").replace(/dev_guinbtn_/gi, "");
			    $.albamon.windowOpen._scroll("/RecruitManager/ProductGuide/Preview?PRDTCode=" + mflag + "&OptPreview=y&ck=10", "", "950", "725");

    function GIB_Read(Al_GI_No, Win_Type, optgcode) {
        var expurl = "";
        if (optgcode) {
            expurl = "&optgf=" + optgcode;
        }
        var url = "/list/gi/mon_gib_read.asp?AL_GI_No=" + Al_GI_No + expurl;
        if (Win_Type == "2") {	//스킨
            url = "/list/gi/mon_gib_read_skin.asp?AL_GI_No=" + Al_GI_No + expurl;
            window.open(url, "mon_gib_read_skin", "width=865,height=700,scrollbars=yes,location=yes");
        } else if (Win_Type == "1") {	//새창
            window.open(url, "", "");
        } else {
            top.location.href = url;
        }
    }
    $(function () {

        //채용 간략보기
        var main_simpleview = $(".pgSimpleGI");
        $(document).on("click", ".pgSimpleGI", function () {
            $('.pgSimpleView').remove();
            $('.dev_optinfolayer').remove();
            $('.pgSimpleViewIfr').remove();
            var al_gi_no = $(this).attr("id").substring(14);
            var optgoodcd = $(this).attr("optgcd");
            var exurl = "";
            if (optgoodcd) {
                exurl = "?optgf=" + optgoodcd;
            }
            $(this).simpleLayerView(al_gi_no, 513, 287, '/Recruit/Home/Preview' + exurl, '', '');
            return false;
        });

        var main_simpleviewGG = $(".pgSimpleGG");
        $(document).on("click", ".pgSimpleGG", function () {
            $('.pgSimpleView').remove();
            $('.dev_optinfolayer').remove();
            $('.pgSimpleViewIfr').remove();
            var m_id = $(this).attr("id").substring(14);
            $(this).simpleLayerView(m_id, 545, 205, '/list/gg/simpleview_gg.asp', '', '');
            return false;
        });

        $("#dev_opt_platinum li:not(.dev_Franchise_c)").each(function () {
            $(this).focusin(function () { $("#dev_opt_platinum li.dev_Franchise_c > div").hide(); });
        });
        $("div#dev_opt_platinum li.dev_Franchise_c").each(function () {
            var ele = $(this);
            ele
			.hover(
					function () { $("> div", ele).show(); }
				, function () { $("> div", ele).hide(); })
			.focusin(function () {
			    $("div#dev_opt_platinum li.dev_Franchise_c").not(this).each(function () {
			        $(" > div", this).hide();
			    });
			    $("> div", ele).show();
			});
        });


        $("#dev_opt_platinum li:not(.dev_Franchise_v)").each(function () {
            $(this).focusin(function () { $("#dev_opt_platinum li.dev_Franchise_v > div").hide(); });
        });
        $("div#dev_opt_platinum li.dev_Franchise_v").each(function () {
            var ele = $(this);
            ele
			.hover(


					function () { $("> div", ele).show(); }
				, function () { $("> div", ele).hide(); })
			.focusin(function () {
			    $("div#dev_opt_platinum li.dev_Franchise_v").not(this).each(function () {
			        $(" > div", this).hide();
			    });
			    $("> div", ele).show();
			})
        });

    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    GrandDraw();
    function GrandDraw() {
        aryGrandG.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
        aryGrand.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });

        var GrandCnt = aryGrandG.length + aryGrand.length;
        var divideNumB = 4;
        var TotalLoopBG = GrandCnt;

        if (GrandCnt % divideNumB > 0)
            TotalLoopBG = (parseInt((GrandCnt / divideNumB)) * divideNumB) + divideNumB;


        var linkType = "";
        var aLink = "";
        var imgLink = "";

        var GrandFormat = [];
        GrandFormat.push("<li {0}>");
        GrandFormat.push("   <dl>");
        GrandFormat.push("       <dt>{1}<span class='logo'>{2}</span></a></dt>");
        GrandFormat.push("       <dd class='tit'>{3}</dd>");
        GrandFormat.push("       <dd class='etc'><span>{4}</span><span class='pay'>{5}</span></dd>");
        GrandFormat.push("       <dd class='bv'>{6}</dd>");
        GrandFormat.push("   </dl>");
        GrandFormat.push("</li>");

        var GrandG = "";
        var Grand = "";

        if (GrandCnt > 0) {
            for (var i = 0; i < aryGrandG.length; i++) {

                GrandG = GrandFormat.join("");
                GrandG = GrandG.replace("{0}", "class='gold'");

                GrandG = GrandG.replace("{1}", aryGrandG[i].strLink + aryGrandG[i].c_name);
                GrandG = GrandG.replace("{2}", aryGrandG[i].strImg);
                GrandG = GrandG.replace("{3}", aryGrandG[i].strSubjectClass);
                GrandG = GrandG.replace("{4}", aryGrandG[i].dutyGuCode);
                GrandG = GrandG.replace("{5}", aryGrandG[i].strPay);
                GrandG = GrandG.replace("{6}", "<button type='button' class='pgSimpleGI smr' id='pgSimpleGraPL_" + aryGrandG[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + aryGrandG[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");

                var $GrandG = $(GrandG);

                $GrandG.appendTo("#grand");

            }

            for (var i = 0; i < aryGrand.length; i++) {

                Grand = GrandFormat.join("");
                Grand = Grand.replace("{0}", "");

                Grand = Grand.replace("{1}", aryGrand[i].strLink + aryGrand[i].c_name);
                Grand = Grand.replace("{2}", aryGrand[i].strImg);
                Grand = Grand.replace("{3}", aryGrand[i].strSubjectClass);
                Grand = Grand.replace("{4}", aryGrand[i].dutyGuCode);
                Grand = Grand.replace("{5}", aryGrand[i].strPay);
                if (aryGrand[i].type != "GF")
                    Grand = Grand.replace("{6}", "<button type='button' class='pgSimpleGI smr' id='pgSimpleGraPL_" + aryGrand[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + aryGrand[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");
                else
                    Grand = Grand.replace("{6}", "");

                var $Grand = $(Grand);

                $Grand.appendTo("#grand");
            }

            for (var i = 0; i < (TotalLoopBG - GrandCnt) ; i++) {
                var $li = $("<li class='none'></li>");
                $li.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Grand&amp;utm_source=blank_banner&amp;utm_medium=click&amp;utm_campaign=grand');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_grand_1.gif' alt='파워점프, 지역Grand, 지역Top-Logo 상품안내 및 신청'/></a>");
                $li.appendTo("#grand");
            }
        }
        else {

            for (var i = 0; i < 4 ; i++) {
                var $li = $("<li class='none'></li>");
                $li.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Grand&amp;utm_source=blank_banner&amp;utm_medium=click&amp;utm_campaign=grand');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_grand_1.gif' alt='파워점프, 지역Grand, 지역Top-Logo 상품안내 및 신청'/></a>");
                $li.appendTo("#grand");
            }

        }
    }
</script>




<!-- Hit알바 -->

<script type="text/javascript">
    var aryHit = new Array();
    var aryHitJK = new Array();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    HitDraw();

    function HitDraw() {
        aryHit.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
        aryHitJK.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });

        var HitCnt = aryHit.length + aryHitJK.length;
        var divideNumB = 3;
        var TotalLoopBG = HitCnt;

        if (HitCnt % divideNumB > 0)
            TotalLoopBG = (parseInt((HitCnt / divideNumB)) * divideNumB) + divideNumB;

        var linkType = "";
        var aLink = "";
        var imgLink = "";

        var HitFormat = [];
        HitFormat.push("<li {0}>");
        HitFormat.push("   <dl>");
        HitFormat.push("       <dt>{1}<span class='logo'>{2}</span></a></dt>");
        HitFormat.push("       <dd class='tit'>{3}</dd>");
        HitFormat.push("       <dd class='etc'><span>{4}</span><span class='pay'>{5}</span></dd>");
        HitFormat.push("       <dd class='bv'>{6}</dd>");
        HitFormat.push("   </dl>");
        HitFormat.push("</li>");

        var Hit = "";
        var HitJ = "";

        if (HitCnt > 0) {
            for (var i = 0; i < aryHit.length; i++) {

                Hit = HitFormat.join("");
                Hit = Hit.replace("{0}", "class='a" + aryHit[i].staticImgNo + "'");
                Hit = Hit.replace("{1}", aryHit[i].strLink + aryHit[i].c_name);
                Hit = Hit.replace("{2}", aryHit[i].strImg);
                Hit = Hit.replace("{3}", aryHit[i].strSubjectClass);
                Hit = Hit.replace("{4}", aryHit[i].dutyGuCode);
                Hit = Hit.replace("{5}", aryHit[i].strPay);
                Hit = Hit.replace("{6}", "<button type='button' class='pgSimpleGI smr' id='pgSimpleHitPL_" + aryHit[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + aryHit[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");

                var $Hit = $(Hit);

                $Hit.appendTo("#hit");

            }

            for (var i = 0; i < aryHitJK.length; i++) {

                HitJ = HitFormat.join("");
                HitJ = HitJ.replace("{0}", "class='a" + aryHitJK[i].staticImgNo + "'");

                aLink = "<a href='" + aryHitJK[i].linkUrl + "' target='_blank'>";
                imgLink = "<img src='" + aryHitJK[i].logoUrl + "' alt='" + aryHitJK[i].c_name + "' />";

                HitJ = HitJ.replace("{1}", aLink + aryHitJK[i].c_name);
                HitJ = HitJ.replace("{2}", imgLink);
                HitJ = HitJ.replace("{3}", aLink + aryHitJK[i].subject + "</a>");
                HitJ = HitJ.replace("{4}", aryHitJK[i].dutyGuCode);
                HitJ = HitJ.replace("{5}", aryHitJK[i].strPay);
                HitJ = HitJ.replace("{6}", aLink + "<button type='button' class='smrjk'><span>새창</span></button></a>");

                var $HitJ = $(HitJ);

                $HitJ.appendTo("#hit");
            }

            for (var i = 0; i < (TotalLoopBG - HitCnt) ; i++) {
                var $li = $("<li class='none'></li>");
                $li.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Hit&amp;utm_source=blank_banner&amp;utm_medium=click&amp;utm_campaign=banner');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_hit_1.gif' alt='점프, 지역Special, 지역 Top, 업직종 Top 무료상품안내 및 신청'/></a>");
                $li.appendTo("#hit");
            }
        }
        else {
            for (var i = 0; i < divideNumB; i++) {
                var $li = $("<li class='none'></li>");
                $li.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Hit&amp;utm_source=blank_banner&amp;utm_medium=click&amp;utm_campaign=banner');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_hit_1.gif' alt='점프, 지역Special, 지역 Top, 업직종 Top 무료상품안내 및 신청'/></a>");
                $li.appendTo("#hit");
            }
        }
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    FocusDraw();
    function FocusDraw() {

        aryFocus.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
        aryFocus_G.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
        var FocusCnt = aryFocus.length + aryFocus_G.length;
        var divideNumB = 3;
        var TotalLoopBG = FocusCnt;

        if (FocusCnt % divideNumB > 0)
            TotalLoopBG = (parseInt((FocusCnt / divideNumB)) * divideNumB) + divideNumB;


        var FocusFormat = [];
        FocusFormat.push("<li {0}>");
        FocusFormat.push("   <dl>");
        FocusFormat.push("       <dt>{1}{2}</a></dt>");
        FocusFormat.push("       <dd class='tit'>{3}</dd>");
        FocusFormat.push("       <dd class='etc'><span>{4}</span><span class='pay'>{5}</span></dd>");
        FocusFormat.push("       <dd class='bv'>{6}</dd>");
        FocusFormat.push("   </dl>");
        FocusFormat.push("</li>");

        var Focus = "";
        var FocusG = "";

        if (FocusCnt > 0) {
            for (var i = 0; i < aryFocus_G.length; i++) {

                FocusG = FocusFormat.join("");
                FocusG = FocusG.replace("{0}", "class='gold'");
                FocusG = FocusG.replace("{1}", aryFocus_G[i].opt_Icon);
                FocusG = FocusG.replace("{2}", aryFocus_G[i].strLink + aryFocus_G[i].c_name);
                FocusG = FocusG.replace("{3}", aryFocus_G[i].strSubjectClass);
                FocusG = FocusG.replace("{4}", aryFocus_G[i].dutyGuCode);
                FocusG = FocusG.replace("{5}", aryFocus_G[i].strPay);
                FocusG = FocusG.replace("{6}", "<button type='button' class='pgSimpleGI smr ' id='pgSimpleFocPL_" + aryFocus_G[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + aryFocus_G[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");

                var $FocusG = $(FocusG);

                $FocusG.appendTo("#focus");

            }

            for (var i = 0; i < aryFocus.length; i++) {
                Focus = FocusFormat.join("");
                Focus = Focus.replace("{0}", "");
                Focus = Focus.replace("{1}", aryFocus[i].opt_Icon);
                Focus = Focus.replace("{2}", aryFocus[i].strLink + aryFocus[i].c_name);
                Focus = Focus.replace("{3}", aryFocus[i].strSubjectClass);
                Focus = Focus.replace("{4}", aryFocus[i].dutyGuCode);

                var $Focus = $(Focus);

                $Focus.appendTo("#focus");

                $li.appendTo("#focus");
            }
        }
        else {
            for (var i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
                var $li = $("<li class='none'></li>");
                $li.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Focus&amp;utm_source=blank_banner&amp;utm_medium=click&amp;utm_campaign=focus','','');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_focus_1.gif'  alt='점프, 지역 TOP 무료 상품안내 및 신청' /></a>");

        }
    }

     SpecialDraw();

     function SpecialDraw() {

         arySpecial_F.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
         arySpecial_G.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
         arySpecial.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
         arySpecial_JK.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });

         var SpecialFormat = [];
         SpecialFormat.push("<tr {0}>");
         SpecialFormat.push("   <td class='area'>{1}</td>");
         SpecialFormat.push("   <td class='sub'>");
         SpecialFormat.push("       <span class='sWrap'>");
         SpecialFormat.push("            {2}"); // img
         SpecialFormat.push("            {3}"); // a
         SpecialFormat.push("            {4}"); // button
         SpecialFormat.push("    </td>");
         SpecialFormat.push("    <td class='cmp'>{5}</td>");
         SpecialFormat.push("    <td class='pay'>{6}</td>");
         SpecialFormat.push("</tr>");

         var SpecialF = "";
         var SpecialG = "";
         var Special = "";
         var SpecialJK = "";
         var SpecialB = "";

         for (var i = 0; i < arySpecial_F.length; i++) {

             SpecialF = SpecialFormat.join("");
             SpecialF = SpecialF.replace("{0}", "class=''");
             SpecialF = SpecialF.replace("{1}", arySpecial_F[i].dutyGuCode);
             SpecialF = SpecialF.replace("{2}", "");

             linkType = 0;
             SpecialF = SpecialF.replace("{3}", arySpecial_F[i].strSubjectClass);
             SpecialF = SpecialF.replace("{4}", "<button type='button' class='pgSimpleGI smr' id='pgSimpleSpePL_" + arySpecial_F[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + arySpecial_F[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");

         }

         for (var i = 0; i < arySpecial_G.length; i++) {

             SpecialG = SpecialG.replace("{6}", arySpecial_G[i].strPay);

             var $SpecialG = $(SpecialG);

             $SpecialG.appendTo("#special");
         }

         for (var i = 0; i < arySpecial.length; i++) {
             Special = SpecialFormat.join("");
             Special = Special.replace("{0}", "");
             Special = Special.replace("{1}", arySpecial[i].dutyGuCode);

     function DrawSpecialBanner(SpecialFormat) {
         arySpecial_B.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });

             SpecialB = SpecialB.replace("{6}", arySpecial_B[i].strPay);

             var $SpecialB = $(SpecialB);

             $SpecialB.appendTo("#special");


         }
     }

<script type="text/javascript">

    DrawBox();
    function DrawBox() {
        aryBox.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });
        aryBoxJK.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });

        var BoxFormat = [];
        BoxFormat.push("<li>");
        BoxFormat.push("   <dl>");
        BoxFormat.push("       <dt>{1}{2}</dt>");
        BoxFormat.push("       <dd class='tit'>{3}</dd>");
        BoxFormat.push("       <dd class='etc'><span>{4}</span><span class='pay'>{5}</span></dd>");
        BoxFormat.push("       <dd class='bv'>{6}</dd>");
        BoxFormat.push("   </dl>");
        BoxFormat.push("</li>");

        var Box = "";
        var BoxJK = "";
        var BoxCnt = 0;

        if (aryBox != null && aryBox.length > 0) {
            for (var i = 0; i < aryBox.length; i++) {

                BoxCnt = BoxCnt + aryBox.length;
                Box = BoxFormat.join("");
                Box = Box.replace("{1}", aryBox[i].opt_Icon);
                Box = Box.replace("{2}", aryBox[i].strLink + aryBox[i].c_name + "</a>");
                Box = Box.replace("{3}", aryBox[i].strSubjectClass);
                Box = Box.replace("{4}", aryBox[i].dutyGuCode);
                Box = Box.replace("{5}", aryBox[i].strPay);
                Box = Box.replace("{6}", "<button type='button' class='pgSimpleGI smr' id='pgSimpleBoxPL_" + aryBox[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + aryBox[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");

                var $Box = $(Box);
                $Box.appendTo("#Box");
            }
        }
        if (aryBoxJK != null && aryBoxJK.length > 0) {
            for (var i = 0; i < aryBoxJK.length; i++) {

                BoxCnt = BoxCnt + aryBoxJK.length;
                BoxJK = BoxFormat.join("");
                aLink = "<a href='" + aryBoxJK[i].guinLink + "' target='_blank'>";
                BoxJK = BoxJK.replace("{1}", aLink + aryBoxJK[i].c_name + "</a>");
                BoxJK = BoxJK.replace("{2}", "");
                BoxJK = BoxJK.replace("{3}", aLink + aryBoxJK[i].subject + "</a>");
                BoxJK = BoxJK.replace("{4}", aryBoxJK[i].dutyGuCode);
                BoxJK = BoxJK.replace("{5}", aryBoxJK[i].strPay);
                BoxJK = BoxJK.replace("{6}", aLink + "<button type='button' class='smrjk' ><span>새창</span></button></a>");

                var $BoxJK = $(BoxJK);

                $BoxJK.appendTo("#Box");

            }
        }

        if (BoxCnt == 0) {
            var $li = $("<li class='none'></li>");
            $li.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Box&amp;utm_source=blank_banner&amp;utm_medium=click&amp;utm_campaign=box','','');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_box_1.gif?1' alt='지역TOP 무료 상품안내 및 신청'/></a>");
            $li.appendTo("#Box");
        }
    }
</script>



    </div>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">

    PointDraw();
    function PointDraw() {

        var TotalCnt = aryPoint.length;
        var divideNumB = 2;
        var TotalLoopB = 0;

        if (TotalCnt % divideNumB > 0)
            TotalLoopB = ((TotalCnt / divideNumB) * divideNumB) + divideNumB;
        else
            TotalLoopB = TotalCnt;

        aryPoint.sort(function () { return Math.random() * 2 - 1; });

        var PointFormat = [];
        PointFormat.push("   <td {6}>{1}</td>");
        PointFormat.push("   <td {7}>");
        PointFormat.push("      <span class='sWrap'>");
        PointFormat.push("         {2}");
        PointFormat.push("         {3}");
        PointFormat.push("         {4}");
        PointFormat.push("         ");
        PointFormat.push("   </td>");
        PointFormat.push("   <td {8}>{5}</td>");


        var Point = "";
        var $tr = $("<tr></tr>");
        var $Point = "";

        if (TotalCnt > 0) {
            for (var i = 0; i < TotalLoopB; i++) {

                if (i < aryPoint.length) {
                    Point = PointFormat.join("");
                    Point = Point.replace("{1}", aryPoint[i].dutyGuCode);
                    Point = Point.replace("{2}", aryPoint[i].opt_Icon);
                    Point = Point.replace("{3}", aryPoint[i].strSubjectClass);
                    Point = Point.replace("{4}", "<button type='button' class='pgSimpleGI smr' id='pgSimplePoiPL_" + aryPoint[i].alGINo + "' optgcd='" + aryPoint[i].clickCount + "'><span>요약</span></button>");



                    if (aryPoint[i].bgColor == "2") {
                        Point = Point.replace("{5}", (aryPoint[i].strLink).replace("<a", "<a class='cmp'") + aryPoint[i].c_name + "</a>");
                        Point = Point.replace("{6}", "class='pbg'");
                        Point = Point.replace("{7}", "class='pbg'");
                        Point = Point.replace("{8}", "class='pbg'");

                    }
                    else {
                        Point = Point.replace("{5}", aryPoint[i].strLink + aryPoint[i].c_name + "</a>");
                        Point = Point.replace("{6}", "");
                        Point = Point.replace("{7}", "");
                        Point = Point.replace("{8}", "");
                    }


                    $Point = $(Point);
                    $Point.appendTo($tr);



                }
                else {

                    $Point = $("<td colspan='3'  class='none'></td>")
                    $Point.html("<a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Point&amp;utm_source=blank_banner&amp;utm_medium=click&amp;utm_campaign=point','','');return false;\"><img src='http://contents.albamon.kr/monimg/main/rent_point_1.gif'  alt='부담없는 비용으로 알바몬 메인광고의 효과를 확인하세요! 상품안내 및 신청' /></a>");
                        $Point.appendTo($tr);
                    }



                    if (i > 0 && (i + 1) % 2 == 0) {
                        $tr.appendTo("#Point");
                        $tr = $("<tr></tr>");
                    }

                }
            }
            else
            {
                $tr.html(" <td colspan='3' class='none'><a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Point&amp;utm_source=blank_banner&amp;utm_medium=click&amp;utm_campaign=point','','');return false;\"><img src='/monimg/main/rent_point_1.gif'  alt='부담없는 비용으로 알바몬 메인광고의 효과를 확인하세요! 상품안내 및 신청' /></a></td><td colspan='3' class='none'><a href='#' onclick=\"javascript:goMainLoc('/RecruitManager/Recruit/Regist-Form?PRDTCode=Point&amp;utm_source=blank_banner&amp;utm_medium=click&amp;utm_campaign=point','','');return false;\"><img src='/monimg/main/rent_point_1.gif'  alt='부담없는 비용으로 알바몬 메인광고의 효과를 확인하세요! 상품안내 및 신청' /></a></td>");
            $tr.appendTo("#Point");
        }
    }

    $(function () {
        $('#dev_MainPoint tr:nth-child(5n)').addClass('dLine');
        $('#dev_MainPoint td:nth-child(2)').addClass('sub');
        $('#dev_MainPoint td:nth-child(3)').addClass('line');
    });

                    <script type="text/javascript">
                        $(document).ready(function () {
                            //Top으로 가기 버튼 제어.
                            $('#dev_topBtn').hide();
                            $(function () {
                                $(window).scroll(function () {
                                    if ($(this).scrollTop() > 0) $('#dev_topBtn').fadeIn(100);
                                    else $('#dev_topBtn').fadeOut(200);
                                    var minTop = $("#footer").offset().top - $("#dev_topBtn").height();
                                    if (minTop <= $("#dev_topBtn").offset().top) {
                                        $("#dev_topBtn").css({ position: "absolute" }).offset({ top: minTop });
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        var bottomHeight = 750;
                                        var winHeight = $(window).height();
                                        bottomHeight = bottomHeight > winHeight ? winHeight : bottomHeight
                                        if ($(document).scrollTop() + $("#dev_topBtn").height() + bottomHeight < $("#dev_topBtn").offset().top) $("#dev_topBtn").css({ position: "fixed", top: "auto" });
                                    }
                                });
                                $('#dev_topBtn a').click(function () {
                                    $('body,html').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 300);
                                    return false;
                                });
                            });
                        });
                    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
    /* js lazy fn */
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
        var scriptEle=document.createElement('script');
        scriptEle.type='text/javascript';
        var loaded=false;
        scriptEle.onreadystatechange=function() {
            // 서버에서 읽어올 경우 loaded, 캐쉬에서 가져올 경우 complete 이기에 둘 모두 처리
            if (this.readyState == 'loaded' || this.readyState == 'complete') {
                if (loaded) return;
                loaded = true;
                callback();
            }
        }
        scriptEle.onload=function() {
            callback();
        };
        scriptEle.src=url;
        document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(scriptEle);
    }

    (function($) {
        $(window).load(function() {
            //google-analytics
            loadScript('/Scripts/js/adcode/google-analytics.js', function () {});
            //DA광고 전환 트래킹
            loadScript('/Scripts/js/adcode/DA_tag.js', function () {});
            loadScript('/Scripts/js/adcode/a_square_2017.js', function () {});

            //Facebook Pixel
            loadScript('/Scripts/js/adcode/Facebook_Pixel.js', function () { FBPixel("", ""); });
        });
    })(jQuery);

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">   

    var DS_UID_Value = "";

    if (window._dslog) {
        window._dslog.setUID(DS_UID_Value);
        window._dslog.dispatch();
    } else {
        var dslog_tag = document.getElementById("dslog_tag");
        if (dslog_tag != null && dslog_tag != undefined) {
            dslog_tag.onload = dslog_tag.onreadystatechange = function () {
                dslog_tag.onload = dslog_tag.onreadystatechange = null;
                window._dslog.setUIDCookie(DS_UID_Value);
                window._dslog.dispatch();
            }
        }
    }
</script>
